│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Agent: Engineering Lead for the engineering team, directing the work of the engineer                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Task: Take the high level requirements described here and prepare a detailed design for the engineer; everything should be in 1 python module, but outline the classes and methods in the   │
│  module. Here are the requirements: A simple account management system for a trading simulation platform.                                                                                    │
│  The system should allow users to create an account, deposit funds, and withdraw funds.                                                                                                      │
│  The system should allow users to record that they have bought or sold shares, providing a quantity.                                                                                         │
│  The system should calculate the total value of the user's portfolio, and the profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                       │
│  The system should be able to report the holdings of the user at any point in time.                                                                                                          │
│  The system should be able to report the profit or loss of the user at any point in time.                                                                                                    │
│  The system should be able to list the transactions that the user has made over time.                                                                                                        │
│  The system should prevent the user from withdrawing funds that would leave them with a negative balance, or                                                                                 │
│  from buying more shares than they can afford, or selling shares that they don't have.                                                                                                       │
│  The system has access to a function get_share_price(symbol) which returns the current price of a share, and includes a test implementation that returns fixed prices for AAPL, TSLA,        │
│  GOOGL.                                                                                                                                                                                      │
│  - Enforce trading rules IMPORTANT: Only output the design in markdown format, laying out in detail the classes and functions in the module, describing the functionality.                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │

╭─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── ✅ Agent Final Answer ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Agent: Engineering Lead for the engineering team, directing the work of the engineer                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Final Answer:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│  # Design for `accounts.py` – Trading Simulation Account Management                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Overview                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  The module `accounts.py` implements a simple account management system for a trading simulation platform. It provides a single class `Account` that manages cash balance, share holdings,   │
│  and transaction history. It interfaces with a function `get_share_price(symbol)` to obtain current market prices for stocks. The module enforces all trading rules (no overdrafts, no       │
│  short selling, sufficient funds for purchases).                                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## External Dependency                                                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  - `get_share_price(symbol: str) -> float` – This function is defined within the module (for simplicity and testability). It returns fixed prices for the following symbols:                 │
│    - `AAPL`: 150.00                                                                                                                                                                          │
│    - `TSLA`: 700.00                                                                                                                                                                          │
│    - `GOOGL`: 2800.00                                                                                                                                                                        │
│    - For any other symbol, it raises a `ValueError`.                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Module Components                                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### 1. Transaction Data Class                                                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```python                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│  from dataclasses import dataclass                                                                                                                                                           │
│  from datetime import datetime                                                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  @dataclass                                                                                                                                                                                  │
│  class Transaction:                                                                                                                                                                          │
│      """Represents a single financial transaction."""                                                                                                                                        │
│      transaction_type: str          # 'deposit', 'withdraw', 'buy', 'sell'                                                                                                                   │
│      symbol: str | None             # stock symbol (None for cash transactions)                                                                                                              │
│      quantity: int                  # number of shares (0 for cash)                                                                                                                          │
│      price: float                   # price per share (0 for cash)                                                                                                                           │
│      total: float                   # total monetary value (positive for credits, negative for debits)                                                                                       │
│      timestamp: datetime            # when the transaction occurred                                                                                                                          │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### 2. `get_share_price` Function                                                                                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```python                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│  def get_share_price(symbol: str) -> float:                                                                                                                                                  │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      Return the current price for a given stock symbol.                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      This is a test implementation returning fixed prices for predefined symbols.                                                                                                            │
│      For any unknown symbol, it raises a ValueError.                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Args:                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│          symbol (str): Stock ticker symbol (e.g., 'AAPL', 'TSLA', 'GOOGL').                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Returns:                                                                                                                                                                                │
│          float: Current price per share.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Raises:                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ValueError: If the symbol is not supported.                                                                                                                                         │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      prices = {                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          'AAPL': 150.00,                                                                                                                                                                     │
│          'TSLA': 700.00,                                                                                                                                                                     │
│          'GOOGL': 2800.00,                                                                                                                                                                   │
│      }                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│      if symbol not in prices:                                                                                                                                                                │
│          raise ValueError(f"Unknown symbol: {symbol}")                                                                                                                                       │
│      return prices[symbol]                                                                                                                                                                   │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### 3. `Account` Class                                                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```python                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│  class Account:                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      A trading simulation account.                                                                                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Manages cash balance, share holdings, and transaction history.                                                                                                                          │
│      Enforces constraints: no negative cash, no short selling, no trading                                                                                                                    │
│      beyond available funds or holdings.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Attributes:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│          balance (float): Current cash balance (>= 0).                                                                                                                                       │
│          holdings (dict[str, int]): Dictionary mapping stock symbol -> quantity owned.                                                                                                       │
│          transactions (list[Transaction]): Chronological list of all transactions.                                                                                                           │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def __init__(self, initial_balance: float = 0.0) -> None:                                                                                                                               │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Create a new account with an optional initial balance.                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              initial_balance (float): Starting cash balance (default 0.0).                                                                                                                   │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def deposit(self, amount: float) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                                        │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Deposit cash into the account.                                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              amount (float): Positive amount to deposit.                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The deposit transaction record.                                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If amount <= 0.                                                                                                                                                     │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def withdraw(self, amount: float) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                                       │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Withdraw cash from the account.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              amount (float): Positive amount to withdraw.                                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The withdrawal transaction record.                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If amount <= 0 or if amount exceeds current balance.                                                                                                                │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def buy(self, symbol: str, quantity: int) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                               │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Buy shares of a stock.                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Uses get_share_price to determine cost. Deducts total cost from balance                                                                                                             │
│          and adds shares to holdings.                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              symbol (str): Stock symbol to buy.                                                                                                                                              │
│              quantity (int): Number of shares (must be positive integer).                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The buy transaction record.                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If quantity <= 0 or if total cost exceeds balance.                                                                                                                  │
│              ValueError: If symbol is unsupported (via get_share_price).                                                                                                                     │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def sell(self, symbol: str, quantity: int) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                              │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Sell shares of a stock.                                                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Uses get_share_price to determine proceeds. Adds proceeds to balance                                                                                                                │
│          and removes shares from holdings.                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              symbol (str): Stock symbol to sell.                                                                                                                                             │
│              quantity (int): Number of shares (must be positive integer).                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The sell transaction record.                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If quantity <= 0, if quantity exceeds held shares,                                                                                                                  │
│                         or if symbol is unsupported (via get_share_price).                                                                                                                   │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_holdings(self) -> dict[str, int]:                                                                                                                                               │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return current holdings (symbol -> shares) as a shallow copy.                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              dict[str, int]: Current shares held.                                                                                                                                            │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_balance(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                         │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return current cash balance.                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Current balance.                                                                                                                                                         │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_portfolio_value(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                 │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Calculate total portfolio value = cash balance + sum(holdings * current price).                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Uses get_share_price for each held symbol.                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Total portfolio value.                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If any held symbol is not supported (should not happen).                                                                                                            │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_profit_loss(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                     │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Calculate profit/loss = current portfolio value - total net deposits.                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Total net deposits = sum of all deposit amounts - sum of all withdrawal amounts.                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Profit (positive) or loss (negative).                                                                                                                                    │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_transactions(self) -> list[Transaction]:                                                                                                                                        │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return a shallow copy of the transaction list (chronological order).                                                                                                                │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              list[Transaction]: All transactions.                                                                                                                                            │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_initial_deposit(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                 │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return the sum of all deposits minus all withdrawals (net cash added).                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Net cash deposits.                                                                                                                                                       │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ...                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Detailed Implementation Notes                                                                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### Internal Helper Methods                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  - `_update_holdings(symbol: str, delta: int) -> None` – Adjust holdings by `delta` (positive for buy, negative for sell). If holdings become 0, remove the entry.                           │
│  - `_record_transaction(t_type: str, symbol: str | None, quantity: int, price: float, total: float) -> Transaction` – Create a `Transaction` with current timestamp, append to               │
│  `transactions`.                                                                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### Validation Rules                                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  - All monetary amounts (`amount`) must be positive.                                                                                                                                         │
│  - `quantity` must be a positive integer.                                                                                                                                                    │
│  - Withdrawal: `amount > balance` → `ValueError`.                                                                                                                                            │
│  - Buy: `quantity * price > balance` → `ValueError`.                                                                                                                                         │
│  - Sell: `symbol not in holdings` or `quantity > holdings[symbol]` → `ValueError`.                                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### Timestamp                                                                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Use `datetime.now()` for each transaction.                                                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ### Example Usage                                                                                                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```python                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│  account = Account()                                                                                                                                                                         │
│  account.deposit(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                                     │
│  account.buy('AAPL', 5)          # Costs 5 * 150 = 750, balance becomes 250                                                                                                                  │
│  account.sell('AAPL', 2)         # Gains 2 * 150 = 300, balance 550, holdings 3                                                                                                              │
│  print(account.get_portfolio_value())  # 550 + (3 * 150) = 1000                                                                                                                              │
│  print(account.get_profit_loss())      # 1000 - 1000 = 0                                                                                                                                     │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Testing                                                                                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  A simple test suite can be written in the same file under `if __name__ == "__main__":` to verify all operations and rules. The test should cover:                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  - Deposit, withdraw, balance changes.                                                                                                                                                       │
│  - Buy and sell shares.                                                                                                                                                                      │
│  - Violations: over‑withdrawal, insufficient funds for buy, selling more shares than held.                                                                                                   │
│  - Portfolio value and profit/loss calculations.                                                                                                                                             │
│  - Transaction history integrity.                                                                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Module‑Level Constants (Optional)                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```python                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│  SUPPORTED_SYMBOLS = frozenset({'AAPL', 'TSLA', 'GOOGL'})                                                                                                                                    │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Error Handling                                                                                                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  All `ValueError` messages should be descriptive, e.g.:                                                                                                                                      │
│  - `"Withdrawal amount 200.0 exceeds current balance 150.0"`                                                                                                                                 │
│  - `"Cannot sell 10 shares of AAPL, only 3 held"`                                                                                                                                            │
│  - `"Buying 10 shares of AAPL costs 1500.0, but balance is 750.0"`                                                                                                                           │
│  - `"Unknown symbol: XYZ"`                                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ## Final Module Structure                                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│  accounts.py                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│  ├── get_share_price()                                                                                                                                                                       │
│  ├── Transaction (dataclass)                                                                                                                                                                 │
│  ├── Account                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│  │   ├── __init__                                                                                                                                                                            │
│  │   ├── deposit                                                                                                                                                                             │
│  │   ├── withdraw                                                                                                                                                                            │
│  │   ├── buy                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│  │   ├── sell                                                                                                                                                                                │
│  │   ├── get_holdings                                                                                                                                                                        │
│  │   ├── get_balance                                                                                                                                                                         │
│  │   ├── get_portfolio_value                                                                                                                                                                 │
│  │   ├── get_profit_loss                                                                                                                                                                     │
│  │   └── get_transactions                                                                                                                                                                    │
│  └── (optional) main test block                                                                                                                                                              │
│  ```                                                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  The module is self‑contained with no third‑party dependencies. All methods are documented with docstrings and type hints. The design is ready for implementation and testing.               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │

│  Task: Write a python module that implements the design described by the engineering lead, in order to achieve the requirements. Here are the requirements: A simple account management      │
│  system for a trading simulation platform.                                                                                                                                                   │
│  The system should allow users to create an account, deposit funds, and withdraw funds.                                                                                                      │
│  The system should allow users to record that they have bought or sold shares, providing a quantity.                                                                                         │
│  The system should calculate the total value of the user's portfolio, and the profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                       │
│  The system should be able to report the holdings of the user at any point in time.                                                                                                          │
│  The system should be able to report the profit or loss of the user at any point in time.                                                                                                    │
│  The system should be able to list the transactions that the user has made over time.                                                                                                        │
│  The system should prevent the user from withdrawing funds that would leave them with a negative balance, or                                                                                 │
│  from buying more shares than they can afford, or selling shares that they don't have.                                                                                                       │
│  The system has access to a function get_share_price(symbol) which returns the current price of a share, and includes a test implementation that returns fixed prices for AAPL, TSLA,        │
│  GOOGL.                                                                                                                                                                                      │
│  - Enforce trading rules                                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
