╭─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── ✅ Agent Final Answer ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Agent: Python Engineer who can write code to achieve the design described by the engineering lead                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  Final Answer:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│  from datetime import datetime                                                                                                                                                               │
│  from dataclasses import dataclass                                                                                                                                                           │
│  from typing import Optional, Dict, List                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  @dataclass                                                                                                                                                                                  │
│  class Transaction:                                                                                                                                                                          │
│      """Represents a single financial transaction."""                                                                                                                                        │
│      transaction_type: str          # 'deposit', 'withdraw', 'buy', 'sell'                                                                                                                   │
│      symbol: Optional[str]          # stock symbol (None for cash transactions)                                                                                                              │
│      quantity: int                  # number of shares (0 for cash)                                                                                                                          │
│      price: float                   # price per share (0 for cash)                                                                                                                           │
│      total: float                   # total monetary value (positive for credits, negative for debits)                                                                                       │
│      timestamp: datetime            # when the transaction occurred                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def get_share_price(symbol: str) -> float:                                                                                                                                                  │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      Return the current price for a given stock symbol.                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      This is a test implementation returning fixed prices for predefined symbols.                                                                                                            │
│      For any unknown symbol, it raises a ValueError.                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Args:                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│          symbol (str): Stock ticker symbol (e.g., 'AAPL', 'TSLA', 'GOOGL').                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Returns:                                                                                                                                                                                │
│          float: Current price per share.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Raises:                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          ValueError: If the symbol is not supported.                                                                                                                                         │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      prices = {                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          'AAPL': 150.00,                                                                                                                                                                     │
│          'TSLA': 700.00,                                                                                                                                                                     │
│          'GOOGL': 2800.00,                                                                                                                                                                   │
│      }                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│      if symbol not in prices:                                                                                                                                                                │
│          raise ValueError(f"Unknown symbol: {symbol}")                                                                                                                                       │
│      return prices[symbol]                                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  class Account:                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      A trading simulation account.                                                                                                                                                           │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Manages cash balance, share holdings, and transaction history.                                                                                                                          │
│      Enforces constraints: no negative cash, no short selling, no trading                                                                                                                    │
│      beyond available funds or holdings.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      Attributes:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│          balance (float): Current cash balance (>= 0).                                                                                                                                       │
│          holdings (dict[str, int]): Dictionary mapping stock symbol -> quantity owned.                                                                                                       │
│          transactions (list[Transaction]): Chronological list of all transactions.                                                                                                           │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def __init__(self, initial_balance: float = 0.0) -> None:                                                                                                                               │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Create a new account with an optional initial balance.                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          If initial_balance > 0, a deposit transaction is automatically recorded.                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              initial_balance (float): Starting cash balance (default 0.0). Must be >= 0.                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If initial_balance < 0.                                                                                                                                             │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          if initial_balance < 0:                                                                                                                                                             │
│              raise ValueError("Initial balance cannot be negative.")                                                                                                                         │
│          self.balance = initial_balance                                                                                                                                                      │
│          self.holdings: Dict[str, int] = {}                                                                                                                                                  │
│          self.transactions: List[Transaction] = []                                                                                                                                           │
│          if initial_balance > 0:                                                                                                                                                             │
│              self._record_transaction('deposit', None, 0, 0.0, initial_balance)                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def _record_transaction(self,                                                                                                                                                           │
│                              t_type: str,                                                                                                                                                    │
│                              symbol: Optional[str],                                                                                                                                          │
│                              quantity: int,                                                                                                                                                  │
│                              price: float,                                                                                                                                                   │
│                              total: float) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                                   │
│          """Create a Transaction with current timestamp, append to transactions list."""                                                                                                     │
│          txn = Transaction(                                                                                                                                                                  │
│              transaction_type=t_type,                                                                                                                                                        │
│              symbol=symbol,                                                                                                                                                                  │
│              quantity=quantity,                                                                                                                                                              │
│              price=price,                                                                                                                                                                    │
│              total=total,                                                                                                                                                                    │
│              timestamp=datetime.now()                                                                                                                                                        │
│          )                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│          self.transactions.append(txn)                                                                                                                                                       │
│          return txn                                                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def _update_holdings(self, symbol: str, delta: int) -> None:                                                                                                                            │
│          """Adjust holdings by delta (positive for buy, negative for sell)."""                                                                                                               │
│          current = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0)                                                                                                                                              │
│          new = current + delta                                                                                                                                                               │
│          if new < 0:                                                                                                                                                                         │
│              # Should not happen if validation is correct, but safeguard                                                                                                                     │
│              raise ValueError(f"Holdings cannot become negative for {symbol}.")                                                                                                              │
│          if new == 0:                                                                                                                                                                        │
│              if symbol in self.holdings:                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  del self.holdings[symbol]                                                                                                                                                   │
│          else:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              self.holdings[symbol] = new                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def deposit(self, amount: float) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                                        │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Deposit cash into the account.                                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              amount (float): Positive amount to deposit.                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The deposit transaction record.                                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If amount <= 0.                                                                                                                                                     │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                                     │
│              raise ValueError("Deposit amount must be positive.")                                                                                                                            │
│          self.balance += amount                                                                                                                                                              │
│          return self._record_transaction('deposit', None, 0, 0.0, amount)                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def withdraw(self, amount: float) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                                       │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Withdraw cash from the account.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              amount (float): Positive amount to withdraw.                                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The withdrawal transaction record.                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If amount <= 0 or if amount exceeds current balance.                                                                                                                │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                                     │
│              raise ValueError("Withdrawal amount must be positive.")                                                                                                                         │
│          if amount > self.balance:                                                                                                                                                           │
│              raise ValueError(                                                                                                                                                               │
│                  f"Withdrawal amount {amount} exceeds current balance {self.balance}"                                                                                                        │
│              )                                                                                                                                                                               │
│          self.balance -= amount                                                                                                                                                              │
│          return self._record_transaction('withdraw', None, 0, 0.0, -amount)                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def buy(self, symbol: str, quantity: int) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                               │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Buy shares of a stock.                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Uses get_share_price to determine cost. Deducts total cost from balance                                                                                                             │
│          and adds shares to holdings.                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              symbol (str): Stock symbol to buy.                                                                                                                                              │
│              quantity (int): Number of shares (must be positive integer).                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The buy transaction record.                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If quantity <= 0 or if total cost exceeds balance.                                                                                                                  │
│              ValueError: If symbol is unsupported (via get_share_price).                                                                                                                     │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                                                   │
│              raise ValueError("Quantity must be a positive integer.")                                                                                                                        │
│          price = get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                                                     │
│          total_cost = price * quantity                                                                                                                                                       │
│          if total_cost > self.balance:                                                                                                                                                       │
│              raise ValueError(                                                                                                                                                               │
│                  f"Buying {quantity} shares of {symbol} costs {total_cost}, but balance is {self.balance}"                                                                                   │
│              )                                                                                                                                                                               │
│          self.balance -= total_cost                                                                                                                                                          │
│          self._update_holdings(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                                             │
│          return self._record_transaction('buy', symbol, quantity, price, -total_cost)                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def sell(self, symbol: str, quantity: int) -> Transaction:                                                                                                                              │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Sell shares of a stock.                                                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Uses get_share_price to determine proceeds. Adds proceeds to balance                                                                                                                │
│          and removes shares from holdings.                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Args:                                                                                                                                                                               │
│              symbol (str): Stock symbol to sell.                                                                                                                                             │
│              quantity (int): Number of shares (must be positive integer).                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              Transaction: The sell transaction record.                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If quantity <= 0, if quantity exceeds held shares,                                                                                                                  │
│                         or if symbol is unsupported (via get_share_price).                                                                                                                   │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                                                   │
│              raise ValueError("Quantity must be a positive integer.")                                                                                                                        │
│          held = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0)                                                                                                                                                 │
│          if quantity > held:                                                                                                                                                                 │
│              raise ValueError(                                                                                                                                                               │
│                  f"Cannot sell {quantity} shares of {symbol}, only {held} held"                                                                                                              │
│              )                                                                                                                                                                               │
│          price = get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                                                     │
│          total_proceeds = price * quantity                                                                                                                                                   │
│          self.balance += total_proceeds                                                                                                                                                      │
│          self._update_holdings(symbol, -quantity)                                                                                                                                            │
│          return self._record_transaction('sell', symbol, quantity, price, total_proceeds)                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_holdings(self) -> Dict[str, int]:                                                                                                                                               │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return current holdings (symbol -> shares) as a shallow copy.                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              dict[str, int]: Current shares held.                                                                                                                                            │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          return dict(self.holdings)                                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_balance(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                         │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return current cash balance.                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Current balance.                                                                                                                                                         │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          return self.balance                                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_portfolio_value(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                 │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Calculate total portfolio value = cash balance + sum(holdings * current price).                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Uses get_share_price for each held symbol.                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Total portfolio value.                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Raises:                                                                                                                                                                             │
│              ValueError: If any held symbol is not supported (should not happen).                                                                                                            │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          total = self.balance                                                                                                                                                                │
│          for symbol, shares in self.holdings.items():                                                                                                                                        │
│              total += get_share_price(symbol) * shares                                                                                                                                       │
│          return total                                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_initial_deposit(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                 │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return the sum of all deposits minus all withdrawals (net cash added).                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Net cash deposits.                                                                                                                                                       │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          net = 0.0                                                                                                                                                                           │
│          for txn in self.transactions:                                                                                                                                                       │
│              if txn.transaction_type == 'deposit':                                                                                                                                           │
│                  net += txn.total                                                                                                                                                            │
│              elif txn.transaction_type == 'withdraw':                                                                                                                                        │
│                  net += txn.total  # txn.total is negative for withdrawals                                                                                                                   │
│          return net                                                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_profit_loss(self) -> float:                                                                                                                                                     │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Calculate profit/loss = current portfolio value - total net deposits.                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              float: Profit (positive) or loss (negative).                                                                                                                                    │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          return self.get_portfolio_value() - self.get_initial_deposit()                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def get_transactions(self) -> List[Transaction]:                                                                                                                                        │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          Return a shallow copy of the transaction list (chronological order).                                                                                                                │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│          Returns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│              list[Transaction]: All transactions.                                                                                                                                            │
│          """                                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          return list(self.transactions)                                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  if __name__ == "__main__":                                                                                                                                                                  │
│      # Simple test suite to verify the class behaviour.                                                                                                                                      │
│      acc = Account()                                                                                                                                                                         │
│      assert acc.get_balance() == 0.0                                                                                                                                                         │
│      assert acc.get_holdings() == {}                                                                                                                                                         │
│      assert acc.get_initial_deposit() == 0.0                                                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │

│      assert acc.get_balance() == 1000.0                                                                                                                                                      │
│      assert txn_dep.transaction_type == 'deposit'                                                                                                                                            │
│      assert txn_dep.total == 1000.0                                                                                                                                                          │
│      assert acc.get_initial_deposit() == 1000.0                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Withdraw                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      txn_wd = acc.withdraw(200.0)                                                                                                                                                            │
│      assert acc.get_balance() == 800.0                                                                                                                                                       │
│      assert txn_wd.transaction_type == 'withdraw'                                                                                                                                            │
│      assert txn_wd.total == -200.0                                                                                                                                                           │

│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Buy                                                                                                                                                                                   │
│      txn_buy = acc.buy('AAPL', 5)   # cost 5 * 150 = 750                                                                                                                                     │
│      assert acc.get_balance() == 50.0                                                                                                                                                        │
│      assert acc.get_holdings() == {'AAPL': 5}                                                                                                                                                │
│      assert txn_buy.transaction_type == 'buy'                                                                                                                                                │
│      assert txn_buy.total == -750.0                                                                                                                                                          │
│      assert acc.get_initial_deposit() == 800.0  # unchanged                                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Sell                                                                                                                                                                                  │
│      txn_sell = acc.sell('AAPL', 2)  # proceeds 2 * 150 = 300                                                                                                                                │
│      assert acc.get_balance() == 350.0                                                                                                                                                       │
│      assert acc.get_holdings() == {'AAPL': 3}                                                                                                                                                │
│      assert txn_sell.transaction_type == 'sell'                                                                                                                                              │
│      assert txn_sell.total == 300.0                                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Portfolio value check                                                                                                                                                                 │
│      # balance = 350, holdings = 3 AAPL @150 -> 450 => total 800                                                                                                                             │
│      assert abs(acc.get_portfolio_value() - 800.0) < 0.001                                                                                                                                   │
│      # P/L = portfolio value - net deposits = 800 - 800 = 0                                                                                                                                  │
│      assert abs(acc.get_profit_loss()) < 0.001                                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Transaction list                                                                                                                                                                      │
│      txns = acc.get_transactions()                                                                                                                                                           │
│      assert len(txns) == 4                                                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Error cases                                                                                                                                                                           │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc.withdraw(500.0)  # only 350 left                                                                                                                                                │
│          assert False, "Should raise ValueError"                                                                                                                                             │
│      except ValueError as e:                                                                                                                                                                 │

│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │

│          assert False, "Should raise ValueError"                                                                                                                                             │
│      except ValueError as e:                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          assert "costs" in str(e) and "balance" in str(e)                                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc.sell('AAPL', 10)  # only 3 held                                                                                                                                                 │
│          assert False, "Should raise ValueError"                                                                                                                                             │
│      except ValueError as e:                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          assert "only" in str(e) and "held" in str(e)                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │

│  Task: Write a gradio UI in a module app.py that demonstrates the given backend class in accounts.py. Assume there is only 1 user, and keep the UI very simple indeed - just a prototype or  │
│  demo. Here are the requirements: A simple account management system for a trading simulation platform.                                                                                      │
│  The system should allow users to create an account, deposit funds, and withdraw funds.                                                                                                      │
│  The system should allow users to record that they have bought or sold shares, providing a quantity.                                                                                         │
│  The system should calculate the total value of the user's portfolio, and the profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                       │
│  The system should be able to report the holdings of the user at any point in time.                                                                                                          │
│  The system should be able to report the profit or loss of the user at any point in time.                                                                                                    │
│  The system should be able to list the transactions that the user has made over time.                                                                                                        │
│  The system should prevent the user from withdrawing funds that would leave them with a negative balance, or                                                                                 │
│  from buying more shares than they can afford, or selling shares that they don't have.                                                                                                       │
│  The system has access to a function get_share_price(symbol) which returns the current price of a share, and includes a test implementation that returns fixed prices for AAPL, TSLA,        │
│  GOOGL.                                                                                                                                                                                      │
│  - Enforce trading rules                                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
