│  import gradio as gr                                                                                                                                                                         │
│  from accounts import Account, get_share_price                                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def create_account(initial_balance):                                                                                                                                                        │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc = Account(initial_balance)                                                                                                                                                      │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  "Account created successfully.")                                                                                                                                            │
│      except Exception as e:                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          return (None, 0.0, "{}", 0.0, 0.0,                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  [], f"Error: {str(e)}")                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def deposit(amount, acc):                                                                                                                                                                   │
│      if acc is None:                                                                                                                                                                         │
│          return (None, 0.0, "{}", 0.0, 0.0, [],                                                                                                                                              │
│                  "Please create an account first.")                                                                                                                                          │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc.deposit(amount)                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  "Deposit successful.")                                                                                                                                                      │
│      except Exception as e:                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  f"Error: {str(e)}")                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def withdraw(amount, acc):                                                                                                                                                                  │
│      if acc is None:                                                                                                                                                                         │
│          return (None, 0.0, "{}", 0.0, 0.0, [],                                                                                                                                              │
│                  "Please create an account first.")                                                                                                                                          │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc.withdraw(amount)                                                                                                                                                                │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  "Withdrawal successful.")                                                                                                                                                   │
│      except Exception as e:                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  f"Error: {str(e)}")                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def buy(symbol, quantity, acc):                                                                                                                                                             │
│      if acc is None:                                                                                                                                                                         │
│          return (None, 0.0, "{}", 0.0, 0.0, [],                                                                                                                                              │
│                  "Please create an account first.")                                                                                                                                          │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc.buy(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                                                           │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  "Purchase successful.")                                                                                                                                                     │
│      except Exception as e:                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  f"Error: {str(e)}")                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def sell(symbol, quantity, acc):                                                                                                                                                            │
│      if acc is None:                                                                                                                                                                         │
│          return (None, 0.0, "{}", 0.0, 0.0, [],                                                                                                                                              │
│                  "Please create an account first.")                                                                                                                                          │
│      try:                                                                                                                                                                                    │
│          acc.sell(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                                                          │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  "Sale successful.")                                                                                                                                                         │
│      except Exception as e:                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          return (acc, acc.get_balance(),                                                                                                                                                     │
│                  str(acc.get_holdings()),                                                                                                                                                    │
│                  acc.get_portfolio_value(),                                                                                                                                                  │
│                  acc.get_profit_loss(),                                                                                                                                                      │
│                  transactions_to_df(acc.get_transactions()),                                                                                                                                 │
│                  f"Error: {str(e)}")                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  def transactions_to_df(txns):                                                                                                                                                               │
│      if not txns:                                                                                                                                                                            │
│          return []                                                                                                                                                                           │
│      data = []                                                                                                                                                                               │
│      for t in txns:                                                                                                                                                                          │
│          data.append([                                                                                                                                                                       │
│              t.transaction_type,                                                                                                                                                             │
│              t.symbol if t.symbol else "",                                                                                                                                                   │
│              t.quantity,                                                                                                                                                                     │
│              t.price,                                                                                                                                                                        │
│              t.total,                                                                                                                                                                        │
│              t.timestamp.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")                                                                                                                                       │
│          ])                                                                                                                                                                                  │
│      return data                                                                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  # Build UI                                                                                                                                                                                  │
│  with gr.Blocks(title="Trading Simulator", theme=gr.themes.Soft()) as demo:                                                                                                                  │
│      gr.Markdown("## 🏦 Simple Trading Account Simulator")                                                                                                                                   │
│      gr.Markdown("Interact with the Account backend. Note: only 1 user (this demo).")                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Current prices display (from get_share_price)                                                                                                                                         │
│      prices_info = f"""                                                                                                                                                                      │
│      **Current share prices (fixed):**                                                                                                                                                       │
│      - AAPL: ${get_share_price('AAPL'):.2f}                                                                                                                                                  │
│      - TSLA: ${get_share_price('TSLA'):.2f}                                                                                                                                                  │
│      - GOOGL: ${get_share_price('GOOGL'):.2f}                                                                                                                                                │
│      """                                                                                                                                                                                     │
│      gr.Markdown(prices_info)                                                                                                                                                                │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Account state                                                                                                                                                                         │
│      account_state = gr.State(None)                                                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Account creation                                                                                                                                                                      │
│      with gr.Row():                                                                                                                                                                          │
│          initial_balance_input = gr.Number(label="Initial Balance", value=0.0)                                                                                                               │
│          create_btn = gr.Button("Create Account")                                                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Account info outputs                                                                                                                                                                  │
│      with gr.Row():                                                                                                                                                                          │
│          with gr.Column(scale=1):                                                                                                                                                            │
│              balance_display = gr.Number(label="Cash Balance", value=0.0)                                                                                                                    │
│              holdings_display = gr.Textbox(label="Holdings", value="{}")                                                                                                                     │
│          with gr.Column(scale=1):                                                                                                                                                            │
│              portfolio_display = gr.Number(label="Portfolio Value", value=0.0)                                                                                                               │
│              pnl_display = gr.Number(label="Profit/Loss", value=0.0)                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Actions                                                                                                                                                                               │
│      gr.Markdown("### Transactions")                                                                                                                                                         │
│      with gr.Row():                                                                                                                                                                          │
│          with gr.Column():                                                                                                                                                                   │
│              deposit_amount = gr.Number(label="Deposit Amount", value=100.0)                                                                                                                 │
│              deposit_btn = gr.Button("Deposit")                                                                                                                                              │
│          with gr.Column():                                                                                                                                                                   │
│              withdraw_amount = gr.Number(label="Withdraw Amount", value=100.0)                                                                                                               │
│              withdraw_btn = gr.Button("Withdraw")                                                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      with gr.Row():                                                                                                                                                                          │
│          with gr.Column():                                                                                                                                                                   │
│              buy_symbol = gr.Dropdown(choices=["AAPL", "TSLA", "GOOGL"], label="Symbol", value="AAPL")                                                                                       │
│              buy_quantity = gr.Number(label="Quantity", value=1, precision=0)                                                                                                                │
│              buy_btn = gr.Button("Buy")                                                                                                                                                      │
│          with gr.Column():                                                                                                                                                                   │
│              sell_symbol = gr.Dropdown(choices=["AAPL", "TSLA", "GOOGL"], label="Symbol", value="AAPL")                                                                                      │
│              sell_quantity = gr.Number(label="Quantity", value=1, precision=0)                                                                                                               │
│              sell_btn = gr.Button("Sell")                                                                                                                                                    │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Transaction history                                                                                                                                                                   │
│      gr.Markdown("### Transaction History")                                                                                                                                                  │
│      transaction_table = gr.Dataframe(                                                                                                                                                       │
│          headers=["Type", "Symbol", "Quantity", "Price", "Total", "Timestamp"],                                                                                                              │
│          datatype=["str", "str", "number", "number", "number", "str"],                                                                                                                       │
│          label="Transactions",                                                                                                                                                               │
│          row_count=10                                                                                                                                                                        │
│      )                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Status messages                                                                                                                                                                       │
│      status_msg = gr.Textbox(label="Status", interactive=False)                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      # Button callbacks                                                                                                                                                                      │
│      create_btn.click(                                                                                                                                                                       │
│          fn=create_account,                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          inputs=[initial_balance_input],                                                                                                                                                     │
│          outputs=[account_state, balance_display, holdings_display,                                                                                                                          │
│                   portfolio_display, pnl_display, transaction_table, status_msg]                                                                                                             │
│      )                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      deposit_btn.click(                                                                                                                                                                      │
│          fn=deposit,                                                                                                                                                                         │
│          inputs=[deposit_amount, account_state],                                                                                                                                             │
│          outputs=[account_state, balance_display, holdings_display,                                                                                                                          │
│                   portfolio_display, pnl_display, transaction_table, status_msg]                                                                                                             │
│      )                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      withdraw_btn.click(                                                                                                                                                                     │
│          fn=withdraw,                                                                                                                                                                        │
│          inputs=[withdraw_amount, account_state],                                                                                                                                            │
│          outputs=[account_state, balance_display, holdings_display,                                                                                                                          │
│                   portfolio_display, pnl_display, transaction_table, status_msg]                                                                                                             │
│      )                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      buy_btn.click(                                                                                                                                                                          │
│          fn=buy,                                                                                                                                                                             │
│          inputs=[buy_symbol, buy_quantity, account_state],                                                                                                                                   │
│          outputs=[account_state, balance_display, holdings_display,                                                                                                                          │
│                   portfolio_display, pnl_display, transaction_table, status_msg]                                                                                                             │
│      )                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      sell_btn.click(                                                                                                                                                                         │
│          fn=sell,                                                                                                                                                                            │
│          inputs=[sell_symbol, sell_quantity, account_state],                                                                                                                                 │
│          outputs=[account_state, balance_display, holdings_display,                                                                                                                          │
│                   portfolio_display, pnl_display, transaction_table, status_msg]                                                                                                             │
│      )                                                                                                                                                                                       │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  if __name__ == "__main__":                                                                                                                                                                  │
│      demo.launch(share=True)                                                                                                                                                                 │

│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def setUp(self):                                                                                                                                                                        │

│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_holdings(), {'AAPL': 10})                                                                                                                             │
│          self.assertEqual(txn.transaction_type, 'buy')                                                                                                                                       │
│          self.assertEqual(txn.symbol, 'AAPL')                                                                                                                                                │
│          self.assertEqual(txn.quantity, 10)                                                                                                                                                  │
│          self.assertEqual(txn.price, 150.0)                                                                                                                                                  │
│          self.assertEqual(txn.total, -1500.0)                                                                                                                                                │
│          self.assertIsInstance(txn.timestamp, datetime)                                                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_multiple_symbols(self):                                                                                                                                                    │
│          self.acc.buy('AAPL', 5)                                                                                                                                                             │
│          self.acc.buy('TSLA', 2)                                                                                                                                                             │
│          expected_holdings = {'AAPL': 5, 'TSLA': 2}                                                                                                                                          │
│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_holdings(), expected_holdings)                                                                                                                        │
│          expected_balance = 10000.0 - (5*150.0 + 2*700.0)                                                                                                                                    │
│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_balance(), expected_balance)                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_insufficient_funds_raises(self):                                                                                                                                           │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError) as cm:                                                                                                                                           │
│              self.acc.buy('GOOGL', 5)  # costs 5*2800 = 14000 > 10000                                                                                                                        │
│          self.assertIn("costs", str(cm.exception))                                                                                                                                           │
│          self.assertIn("balance", str(cm.exception))                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_zero_quantity_raises(self):                                                                                                                                                │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError):                                                                                                                                                 │
│              self.acc.buy('AAPL', 0)                                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_negative_quantity_raises(self):                                                                                                                                            │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError):                                                                                                                                                 │
│              self.acc.buy('AAPL', -1)                                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_unknown_symbol_raises(self):                                                                                                                                               │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError) as cm:                                                                                                                                           │
│              self.acc.buy('XYZ', 1)                                                                                                                                                          │
│          self.assertIn("Unknown symbol", str(cm.exception))                                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_exact_balance(self):                                                                                                                                                       │
│          self.acc.buy('AAPL', 66)  # 66*150 = 9900 <= 10000                                                                                                                                  │
│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_balance(), 100.0)                                                                                                                                     │
│          # Additional buy that uses remaining balance                                                                                                                                        │
│          self.acc.buy('AAPL', 0)  # not allowed                                                                                                                                              │
│          # Buy with exact remaining?                                                                                                                                                         │
│          # 100 / 150 => 0.66 shares not allowed, so can't buy fractional.                                                                                                                    │
│          # Intentionally no further buy.                                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_updates_holdings_correctly(self):                                                                                                                                          │
│          self.acc.buy('TSLA', 3)                                                                                                                                                             │
│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_holdings(), {'TSLA': 3})                                                                                                                              │
│          self.acc.buy('TSLA', 2)                                                                                                                                                             │
│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_holdings(), {'TSLA': 5})                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │

│  class TestPortfolioAndProfit(unittest.TestCase):                                                                                                                                            │
│      """Tests for portfolio value, initial deposit, profit/loss."""                                                                                                                          │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def setUp(self):                                                                                                                                                                        │
│          self.acc = Account()                                                                                                                                                                │
│          self.acc.deposit(5000.0)                                                                                                                                                            │
│          self.acc.buy('AAPL', 10)   # 10 * 150 = 1500                                                                                                                                        │
│          self.acc.buy('TSLA', 2)    # 2 * 700 = 1400                                                                                                                                         │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_portfolio_value(self):                                                                                                                                                         │
│          # cash = 5000 - 1500 - 1400 = 2100                                                                                                                                                  │
│          # holdings value = 10*150 + 2*700 = 1500 + 1400 = 2900                                                                                                                              │
│          # total = 2100 + 2900 = 5000                                                                                                                                                        │
│          self.assertAlmostEqual(self.acc.get_portfolio_value(), 5000.0, places=2)                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_initial_deposit_total(self):                                                                                                                                                   │
│          self.assertEqual(self.acc.get_initial_deposit(), 5000.0)                                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_profit_loss_zero(self):                                                                                                                                                        │
│          self.assertAlmostEqual(self.acc.get_profit_loss(), 0.0, places=2)                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_profit_loss_after_price_change(self):                                                                                                                                          │
│          # With current implementation, price is fixed, so profit/loss only                                                                                                                  │
│          # changes if we deposit/withdraw/buy/sell.                                                                                                                                          │
│          # Simulate a sell at profit: buy low, sell high? But prices are fixed.                                                                                                              │
│          # Actually profit/loss = current value - net deposits.                                                                                                                              │
│          # If we sell after buying, the cash changes, but holdings change.                                                                                                                   │
│          # With fixed prices, no P/L from trades.                                                                                                                                            │
│          # We can test with deposit/withdraw.                                                                                                                                                │
│          self.acc.withdraw(200.0)                                                                                                                                                            │
│          # net deposit now = 5000 - 200 = 4800                                                                                                                                               │
│          # portfolio value = cash after withdraw? balance = 2100 -200 = 1900? Wait: after buy, balance 2100. Withdraw 200 => 1900.                                                           │
│          # holdings value unchanged = 2900 => total = 4800.                                                                                                                                  │
│          # profit/loss = portfolio value - net deposits = 4800 - 4800 = 0.                                                                                                                   │
│          self.assertAlmostEqual(self.acc.get_profit_loss(), 0.0, places=2)                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_mixed_holdings_portfolio_value(self):                                                                                                                                          │
│          # Add another buy                                                                                                                                                                   │
│          self.acc.buy('GOOGL', 1)  # would cost 2800, but balance is 2100, insufficient. So skip.                                                                                            │
│          pass                                                                                                                                                                                │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_portfolio_value_no_holdings(self):                                                                                                                                             │
│          acc = Account(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│          self.assertAlmostEqual(acc.get_portfolio_value(), 1000.0, places=2)                                                                                                                 │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_portfolio_value_multiple_holdings(self):                                                                                                                                       │
│          # Already covered in setUp                                                                                                                                                          │

│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_transaction_ordering(self):                                                                                                                                                    │
│          self.acc.deposit(500.0)                                                                                                                                                             │
│          self.acc.withdraw(200.0)                                                                                                                                                            │
│          self.acc.buy('AAPL', 3)                                                                                                                                                             │
│          txns = self.acc.get_transactions()                                                                                                                                                  │
│          types = [t.transaction_type for t in txns]                                                                                                                                          │
│          self.assertEqual(types, ['deposit', 'deposit', 'withdraw', 'buy'])                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_get_transactions_returns_copy(self):                                                                                                                                           │
│          txns = self.acc.get_transactions()                                                                                                                                                  │

│          self.assertEqual(len(self.acc.get_transactions()), 1)                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │

│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│  class TestAccountEdgeCases(unittest.TestCase):                                                                                                                                              │
│      """Tests for edge cases and boundary conditions."""                                                                                                                                     │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_operations_with_zero_balance(self):                                                                                                                                            │
│          acc = Account()                                                                                                                                                                     │
│          # deposit then withdraw all                                                                                                                                                         │
│          acc.deposit(100.0)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          acc.withdraw(100.0)                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_balance(), 0.0)                                                                                                                                            │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_holdings(), {})                                                                                                                                            │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError):                                                                                                                                                 │
│              acc.withdraw(1.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_buy_and_sell_all_shares(self):                                                                                                                                                 │
│          acc = Account(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│          acc.buy('AAPL', 6)   # cost 900                                                                                                                                                     │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_balance(), 100.0)                                                                                                                                          │
│          acc.sell('AAPL', 6)                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_balance(), 1000.0)                                                                                                                                         │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_holdings(), {})                                                                                                                                            │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_multiple_buys_same_symbol_accumulates(self):                                                                                                                                   │
│          acc = Account(10000.0)                                                                                                                                                              │
│          acc.buy('TSLA', 2)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          acc.buy('TSLA', 3)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_holdings(), {'TSLA': 5})                                                                                                                                   │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_sell_removes_symbol_when_zero(self):                                                                                                                                           │
│          acc = Account(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│          acc.buy('AAPL', 1)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          self.assertIn('AAPL', acc.get_holdings())                                                                                                                                           │
│          acc.sell('AAPL', 1)                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          self.assertNotIn('AAPL', acc.get_holdings())                                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_initial_deposit_after_trades(self):                                                                                                                                            │
│          acc = Account(500.0)                                                                                                                                                                │
│          acc.deposit(200.0)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          acc.withdraw(100.0)                                                                                                                                                                 │
│          self.assertEqual(acc.get_initial_deposit(), 600.0)                                                                                                                                  │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_profit_loss_with_trades(self):                                                                                                                                                 │
│          # Since prices are fixed, no profit/loss from trading itself.                                                                                                                       │
│          # But we can test that net deposit changes profit/loss.                                                                                                                             │
│          acc = Account(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│          acc.buy('AAPL', 5)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          # net deposit = 1000, portfolio value = cash (1000-750=250) + 5*150 = 750 => 1000                                                                                                   │
│          self.assertAlmostEqual(acc.get_profit_loss(), 0.0, places=2)                                                                                                                        │
│          # Withdraw 500? can't, only 250 cash. Deposit additional.                                                                                                                           │
│          acc.deposit(500.0)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          # net deposit = 1500, portfolio value = (250+500=750) + 750 = 1500                                                                                                                  │
│          self.assertAlmostEqual(acc.get_profit_loss(), 0.0, places=2)                                                                                                                        │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_negative_holdings_not_possible(self):                                                                                                                                          │
│          acc = Account(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│          acc.buy('AAPL', 5)                                                                                                                                                                  │
│          # internal _update_holdings should not allow negative, but it's safeguarded                                                                                                         │
│          # we can try through sell more than held, which raises.                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                                                                              │
│      def test_get_share_price_unknown_symbol_in_buy_or_sell(self):                                                                                                                           │
│          acc = Account(1000.0)                                                                                                                                                               │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError):                                                                                                                                                 │
│              acc.buy('UNKNOWN', 1)                                                                                                                                                           │
│          with self.assertRaises(ValueError):                                                                                                                                                 │
│              acc.sell('UNKNOWN', 1)                                                                                                                                                          │
